                   President of the World Peace and Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon Jo

The 62nd Anniversary Speech of the Teacher
 What should I talk about? Looking at your faces, they are truly beautiful. "Thank you" (applause) Every time I see a person's face, I always think, 'Could God have made a person any better than this?' When I think about people, I wonder if it would have been possible to create someone better than the current human being. So, I thought about making the eyes rounder, the nose more prominent, the mouth like this, and even the ears upside down, and I pondered a lot. However, no matter how much I think about it, I conclude that it would not be possible to create anyone better than the current human being. I am a mysterious masterpiece.

Therefore, when you look at people's faces, some might wonder why my face looks like this. Especially for women, there might be those who feel disheartened thinking, 'Why don't I look more beautiful?' But do not think that way. You must realize that to create just one of me, God put in so much effort and concentrated all His thoughts to create this masterpiece.

Even when looking at those who are considered unattractive, each has its own characteristics. There are only four basic features on the face, but when you see how they harmonize, it reflects the myriad forms of beauty. Now, if you put these four features on a signboard, there are 4 billion people in the world, and none of them are the same. How mysterious is that? Think about the 4 billion people. When you consider that, it is truly miraculous. There is no miracle like this. Just think about how hard it would be to create that! (laughter)

And if you look at people with an interest in their faces, you will realize that people cannot be angry, complain, or feel despondent. If you know that the faces of 4 billion people are different and you examine each individual, it is truly mysterious. Therefore, should we not live with the pride of being a masterpiece of such mysterious harmony? If you think that way… don’t you think so? "I think so."

Now, when a person is born as a woman, what would happen if there were only women? (laughter) No matter how beautiful women are, what good is it without men? If there are no men, women would not bother to put on makeup, no matter how much they are taught to do so every day. (laughter) So, the biggest event in the world is likely the absence of men before women. There cannot be a bigger event than this. (laughter)

If there is only one man in a world of nearly 2 billion women, what would happen? Then, a war would break out among women to have that man. It would be a fierce battle. (laughter) That’s right. What would women say about that man? They would spare no means or methods and would invest everything to occupy him in a historical event. Women do not like war, do they? "Yes." Then, would they just sit still, or would they fight to possess that man? (laughter) They can think that way.

On the other hand, if there is only one woman in a world of men, what would happen? "They fight." (laughter) When you think about these things, it is a miracle that you can live with a free heart, not fighting or worrying about such issues, choosing a partner among many men and many women.

Now, if some countries were inhabited only by men, and some only by women, what would happen? (laughter) Moreover, if we consider childbirth, it is all about men… The Bible and Christian thought mainly reflect this, right? Eastern people desire to have sons. What would happen if only boys were born? Do Western women, American women, prefer to have daughters or sons? What do they prefer? "Both." Which one do they want more? "Sons." 

If Western women want sons, and Eastern women also want sons, what would happen if all they had were sons? When women are full, they would all pray, 'God, let me have a son,' and if that prayer is answered, what would happen to this world? If God only allowed sons to be born, what would happen? (laughter) Therefore, no matter how much they pray, God does not grant such requests. It should not be granted. When you think about it, a wise person would not even need to pray for that.

For this reason, even if people give birth freely, the number of men and women worldwide is similar. It is similar. That is mysterious. Therefore, the very fact that people live on this planet is mysterious and miraculous. It is mysterious. The mysterious and miraculous things are those that humans cannot control. This conclusion emerges. Don’t you think so?

Unification Church members must create a vibration of love.

The more ideal a person is, the higher their ideals, the more they desire the mysterious. Isn’t that so? Next, they desire miracles. Then, if the very existence of humanity is mysterious and miraculous, it is happiness that we live seeing things more precious and better than this. Meeting that woman and that man means that I am facing a mysterious man or woman; think about it that way.

Now, there is a power plant of thought, a broadcasting station of thought, and the wavelength of thought is different for everyone. Think about that. It creates harmony. It is not conflict; it is harmony. This vibration is not just a vibration that seeks harmony among white people. It is a vibration that seeks harmony throughout the world. This vibration harmonizes with Eastern people, black people, and all races.

However, when human history is all about blocking and eliminating this, isn’t that a crime? When viewed this way, Christianity is also limited. 'You must go this way. You must go this way,' they say, and they think, 'America must be like this, Japan must be like this,' and they all say that. What is good? Shouldn’t humanity pursue a historical context where all vibrations can resonate? This conclusion emerges.

So, who are those people in this world? Where are those people? That is the problem. Should we only focus on the earthly realm and cut off the spiritual realm when creating vibrations, or should we reach out in all directions? We should reach out in all directions. Everyone would agree with that.

Today, when we look at it, where are the individuals, nations, or organizations that can have such vibrations that think about both the world and the spiritual realm? If such places exist, wouldn’t you want to go there? "We have already found it."

When viewed this way, what is the Unification Church, what is Moon, and what is Reverend Moon doing? Today, on the anniversary of the True Parents, they have placed Eastern people in the Western world. What is this? What is this? (laughter) They have placed Eastern people right in the middle of the Western world, and what are the Western people doing? What is going on here? (laughter)

Let me tell you one thing, and remember this: for an Eastern person to come to Western society and do such work is historically significant, and Reverend Moon is a representative figure in this regard. Reverend Moon has taken these young people and made them not fall away even when they are asked to do more than their parents or their country requires, and even when they undergo deprogramming, they are able to come back.

What is the reason for that? "Love." What is that love? Is it love or is it a robber? "Love!" The problem is different. The vibration that appeared in the East resonates even to the West. Religion is like that. Among religions, the Unification Church is a strange religion. Recently, when some newspapers like the [New York Daily] and [Philadelphia Bulletin] went bankrupt, Reverend Moon created the [Washington Times]. What is this! (applause)

Then, is Reverend Moon a Westerner? "Ah—an Easterner!" They think, "A Westerner is great, but an Easterner? Huh!" They are all falling down now, so why should Reverend Moon be like this? Their companies are for their organizations or individuals, but they cannot connect to a global level beyond a national level. It is different. No matter how big they are, that is all they can grow.

So, when they are threatened and invaded, they naturally retreat, but we are not like that. Because we set the standard for nations and the world, even if our individual selves are invaded and our organization is attacked, we shall advance! Amen! If we fall while going, someone will come out and go again, and if we fall again, someone will come out and go again, and we will continue to advance; we will not retreat. Do you think so? "Yes." Even when looking at the cultural world, the cultural creation of Western society has hit a limit and has now entered a state of bankruptcy, but we can step on this and leap forward. That is wonderful.

So, when we think about this, should the members of the Unification Church go comfortably while the surrounding countries and societies are corrupting and entering a state of bankruptcy, or should we carry a more difficult cross? This issue arises. Even if the path ahead is more miserable than now, we shall advance more fiercely. Amen! "Amen!" (applause) This conclusion emerges.

From this perspective, what path should the members of the Unification Church take? We must create this vibration everywhere in the world, and our vibration must reach to heaven and earth. Think about how wonderful that is. That is the introduction. (laughter) Do you understand what I mean? That is the world.

True Parents are the ones who create the vibration of love.

Now, regarding Reverend Moon of the Unification Church, today is the 62nd anniversary, and we are commemorating it, but we must clarify who Reverend Moon really is.

What is the image of Reverend Moon or Mother, True Parents? What kind of image is this? It is simple. In the historical era, when all people from the past, present, and future create this one vibration, they must all harmonize and act as a core. Isn’t that the position True Parents can hold? It is needed for nations, individuals, families, the East, the West, the spiritual realm, and the earthly world forever.

Then, what kind of vibration is this? That is the question. Think about it as a vibration for making money. If that is the case, it does not resonate in poor worlds, especially in regions like Africa. Yes, centered on America, it may be possible, but it is impossible in underdeveloped countries.

Next, is it a vibration for power? "No." It is only needed in the world of power; it is not needed for the weak, for those without power. Then, would you try to create a vibration centered on knowledge? "No." It may resonate with smart people, but it does not resonate with ignorant people.

When you look at it this way, no matter what you look at, it tilts. No matter what you look at, it tilts. Whether you look at power, money, or knowledge, it tilts. Then, what should this vibration be for? "Love." There is so much love in America. How many kinds of love are there in America? "True love." Have you seen true love? You might not know if Reverend Moon is a fraud. "He is not." How do you know? How do you know? "God knows."

You all might think that I just sit here and control all of you, using you all. (laughter) Why are you laughing? People think that way. It is a fact.

If Reverend Moon has caused a significant event in history, what is it? It is creating a history where parents kidnap their children. How scary and fearful an event is that! Think about how scary and fearful that event is. On the other hand, it is also a wonderful and happy event. It is one or the other. What do you think? It is strange, isn’t it? Parents who take their children away are worried and anxious, but those who are taken away are happy from morning till night. (laughter) When you tell them to go to their mom and dad, they stick to the Unification Church wall. (applause) When you see that, who do you think is doing well? "Unification Church members."

When you are kidnapped and brainwashed and trying to escape over the wall, do you think the spiritual realm would say, 'Do well, do well!' or would they say, 'Hey, you little brat! Catch him, catch him!'? What would they say? "The first one." Would they be on the side of the Unification Church or the opposite side? Where would they be? "On the side of the Unification Church." You are saying that because you are on the side of the Unification Church, but is that really true? "Yes." Then am I proud of that? "Yes." That is how it is.

When viewed this way, it is a miraculous event that someone from the East came and created this vibration in Western society, harmonizing it.

And regarding the Unification Church, high-ranking religious leaders in America and the highest…
Aren't all the people in power opposed to this? Isn't that right? That's right, isn't it? But what's interesting is that in the world, theologians are ranked higher than pastors and elders of Christianity, and scholars are ranked higher than politicians. In the religious world, theologians hold the highest position, but the people who hold real power are currently the power elite and church administrators. However, we must recognize that above them are the scholars. 

As the vibrations spread from the world of scholars, what has our Unification Church done until now? The power elite, who are in the middle tier, oppose us, but we have laid the groundwork that the world of scholars can support. (Applause) It is probably the first time that a religious leader from the East has gathered world scholars like this and is moving the East-West world in this way.

So when those people start writing, they will be writing about the Unification Church and Reverend Moon, and we must understand that we have reached a stage where the most authoritative scholars can write about it, rather than just literary figures. The content of their books will center around praise, controlling this, expanding it, and unifying it globally. The fact that movements centered around such content have begun to emerge all over the world is a mysterious event, a miraculous event. As a result, it has become the core of a new direction for the 4 billion people of the world, especially in the scholarly world.

In North America, in the U.S., they are making a fuss about Reverend Moon, but in South America, the national president is welcoming us and calling our members to ask for help in ideologically arming his military. Among the educated people, there are many members of the Communist Party. Some of their reflections mention that they were in the Communist Party but realized that it was bad and transitioned away from it. Seeing such realities has given them a shocking impression, and the president himself is now welcoming our educational personnel. (Applause)

The president and the administrative leaders have become this way, but when I asked a scholar, what did the scholar say? The scholar said, "President, why are you so late? You should have done this already!" (Laughter) The fact that the president himself is so moved and when he inquires of scholars, the scholars have already laid the groundwork to question the president is an astonishing fact. 

Now, I am nothing, but wherever I go, if I say, "Oh, gather such and such scholars from the scholarly world!" they can gather, can't they? "Yes, they can." Recently, while I was in Germany, I was hiding. They kept wanting to meet, so I was hiding. In the scholarly world, Reverend Moon is a mystery. Normally, they would come to meet if they wanted to see me, but they are not coming... 

Even while living like that, the influence of that vibration is indeed growing. Even in this gathering of scholars or theologians, what do they commonly talk about? They say that once you connect with this organization, you cannot sever that connection. There is a charm to it. They say if you don’t go, you become curious. They cannot forget about our Unification Church or the people of the Unification Church. 

When the New York Times or the Washington Post mentions Reverend Moon, they do not refer to him as a religious revivalist but as a leader of the Korean economy, and that is indeed the reality. This is the problem. 

In terms of culture, recently in New York, famous entertainers could not go to the Little Angels, and there was competition over that, right? A world-famous dancer is saying they need to create Asian dancers. They are not trying to create world dancers but Asian dancers. (Applause) They are talking about old stories as propaganda. 

So what should the image of Reverend Moon, the True Parents of today, be? This is the question. 

Before you think of the image of the True Parents, you must think about what the image of God is. Who is God? He is the parent of humanity, the parent of humanity, and that is the conclusion. Among humanity, there are countless images. Is that easy? 

Even for the extremely irritable white woman, you must become a parent. (Laughter) She is full of complaints and is very... Eastern people may not talk much, but Westerners talk a lot, blabbering away. To be a father to such women, can you just talk? You can only like them by looking at their faces. (Making a facial expression, laughter) 

There are all kinds of people: the good, the bad, the rich, the poor, the sick, the dying, and those who commit suicide. There are all kinds of people. So even if all those people are matched up, God must have the subjectivity necessary to match their talents. He is the parent. Do you think that is easy? "No." I find it very, very easy. (Laughter) 

When you think that way, what kind of path has Reverend Moon walked until now? You would want to know that, right? "Yes." 

To live in the Kingdom of Heaven, one must go through the lower classes. 

Now, did I not have a youthful time full of hope, just like you? "Yes, you did." (Laughter) What was it like back then? Before I knew this purpose, I thought about becoming a friend to the poor in the neighborhood. I was interested in those who were struggling. Even if there were children, I did not try to befriend the children of the wealthy families in the neighborhood. I lived the opposite life. 

If there was someone in the neighborhood who was struggling and could not eat, I would stay awake and do whatever it took to help them. I thought I should become a friend to everyone and go beyond just being a friend. 

You all, before your thirties, want to wear nice clothes, want to show off your appearance, want to be handsome, want to be beautiful, right? I, on the other hand, did not buy new clothes. I went to second-hand stores and bought all dirty clothes. And I intentionally styled my hair like this. While doing that, I walked my own path. My path is different. I tried not to talk much. When I spoke, I knew that I was theoretical, and no one could surpass me. I was organizing myself as if I were someone who did not know anything. 

During my youth, I went everywhere, from the slums to the labor sites. I even lived in beggar's dens. I chased after places like brothels as well. 

During my student days in Tokyo during the Japanese colonial period, on rainy days, I wore student clothes, but I would try to be near the damp workers. I would go to the smelliest places. 

What would I think? I would think, "If this person were my brother or my father, what would it be like? If they are standing in such a miserable state for me, what should I do?" I thought like this. 

And on the tram, I would look at well-dressed students, the so-called smart male and female students, and compare myself. While your laughter flows with your youth and your life flows away, I thought that in my gloomy thoughts, my life would shine, and the sun of hope for the future would rise. I believed that my future was guaranteed and hopeful, while you had no hope for the future. 

You must understand that it is extremely difficult to establish the name of the True Parents throughout one’s life. I had to discover myself, who could possess the subjectivity to be the parent of all people. Therefore, for the not-so-distant future of paradise, I had to go through the life of the lower class, the middle class, and then to the life of the upper class... Do you understand? 

When you look at it this way, it is a pity. Reverend Moon is a pitiful person. No one knows. No one knew me. Friends did not know me, parents did not know me, and siblings did not know me. Even my wife does not know. My mother lives with me now, but she will not know about my father, who will go later. Do you understand what I mean? That is why, having been born as a human in the human world, I am indeed a representative who has wandered around looking for the deep valleys that humans can experience. 

Just by walking that path, I can be a person who deserves sympathy, but there is an increase in persecution along that path. There is an increase in persecution. This is an unavoidable fact. Even when I go back to my hometown, I am an innocent person, but I have become a man who cannot freely visit day or night. I have not committed any sins. 

That person could just study and help the village prosper and improve the neighborhood, but instead, I am in and out of prison and causing problems. 

I really liked my mother. I only talked to her about such things and did not talk about it to anyone else. Then I would go to my ancestors' graves and pray, saying everything. I do not know my path. You know it because you are in the spirit world; you will know my path. 

So, all the neighborhoods, towns, and countries are opposed to me. And the entire Christian world is not without problems. Pastors and elders have said that heresies have arisen and have made strange claims... So all the people connected to me have become the focus of attention. 

When I enter a neighborhood, there are people in the local tavern who do not want to see me, and there are people in restaurants who do not want to see me. Do you understand what I mean? Yet, I am not a bad person. I laid the groundwork in such an environment. 

Making friends and forming a group there is not easy. That is why the spirit world cooperates. If you look at the history of the early Unification Church, all of it was evangelized from the spirit world. It was evangelized from the spirit world. Now, there are many elderly grandmothers in the Unification Church in Korea, but those grandmothers were all evangelized from the spirit world and met with me; I did not evangelize them. 

My sleeping arrangements were not comfortable, and I could not live freely. I always lived in the shade, under the shade. 

When I see that, how much I must have envied the current state of America and the world! You are in heaven, heaven. Even while being in such a place, even though you could be close to heaven, I see that you are in a position where you can run ahead of me in loyalty to heaven, yet you are like this... 

To establish a new tradition, you must sweat and toil. 

Now, when you look at your own position in America and my position, you must understand that I am in a more difficult position than you. Is that right or not? "Yes." Yet you all want to be indebted to me. No one wants to make me indebted to them. Is that right or not? How is it? "Yes." 

Then why does Reverend Moon have to think this way? Knowing such things, why must Reverend Moon walk this path? "Are you talking about walking the path of suffering?" Knowing that position, why does Reverend Moon have to maintain this position and carry this burden? It is because of the name of the True Parents. 

From that perspective, if there is a representative among men, I will not yield to that representative. I have come this far with the belief that "the day I touch it, I will not yield to you in that direction." From then on, I have been able to invest my sincerity as much as I want. I am doing such work now. 

So, centered around the path of indemnity and restoration, I have gone through individual indemnity, family, tribe, nation, and national indemnity, and I have completed the first 3rd 7-year course and established the home church system, and on top of that, I have set the second 3rd 7-year course. This is a historical achievement. As a result, I have finally created a base to settle on the earth, and from now on, we have entered a new era of attacks against the evil world, and you must understand this. 

Until now, we have received numerous attacks, numerous attacks. However, in attacking, it is not to take revenge but to save them. The purpose is different. That is different. Do you understand what I mean? Our opponents are trying to kill Reverend Moon and this organization, but what we are opposing and attacking now is to save them. That is different. 

The FBI is trying to kill the innocent Unification Church, trying to eliminate it, and when we ask for the contents of their investigation to be released, the whole world said it could not be done. An event in history is unfolding where, by the Supreme Court's ruling, they say, "Give it to us!" (Applause) You all know how much they have manipulated to try to catch Reverend Moon. 

When they say we brainwash or do something, it is all to push us into a corner. It is a lie. They investigated, but they could not find evidence for such content. Did I make young people into slaves and exploit them? I am the one being exploited. 

We must be bold. We must proudly boast of our amazing name. You must understand this. "Amen." (Applause) And we must proudly boast of being members of the Unification Church. Members of the Unification Church must proudly boast. We should not boast of ourselves but of the Unification Church. And in the future, we must boast of the ideology of the Unification Church. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Are you not ashamed of being a member? You little brats? "No." What do you mean no? What do you mean no? "No." There are so many who are ashamed right now, you little brats! When they say something, they grab you and ask you to present evidence from the roadside. Now that we have all the materials of the nation and the world, we can confidently catch such people on the street. (Applause) 

Until now, I have lived in the shade without speaking, but my conviction has been strong. I will create such days, and at such times, I will prepare my posture and step forward with my original posture, and I have endured. When I went to prison, I became a parent to those who were living in prison, and when I went to the labor sites, I became a parent to the workers. 

I spent seven years on a boat in Gloucester, America, but I did so with that heart. Even when everyone was taking a nap on the New Hope boat, I did not sleep. When morning came and it was time to sail, if the captain was dozing off, I would wake him up, saying, "Hey, wake up!" I have laid down on the boat once, in the cabin where there was a bed, because I had a headache, but after that, I never did again. It is that hard. There is a responsibility to establish the tradition of all the sailors crossing the ocean. I see it as a responsibility as a parent. 

As you know, to go back and forth to the Unification Industry I created takes about three to four hours. It was common to go twice a day, and there were countless times when I went three times. I have often stopped by three times.
I attended the Unification Theological Seminary for three years, living that way. I went every day. If I wanted to go, I went every day. If I came back late from somewhere, I would go the next morning. Why would I go? I go with sincerity, with sincerity. 

I must say that I will take responsibility for building a global foundation with my own hands. Yet, there are all sorts of people who join the Unification Church and say they won't do fundraising or won't engage in home church activities. These kids! When it comes to selecting who the true Munis are, can I really say I am a true Muni? The very first ancestor of Muni is Reverend Moon, right? "Yes." Those who follow Reverend Moon are not just a bunch of slackers like you. You must understand that they are not beggars. 

In America, I must take responsibility for the most difficult things. Therefore, I must be the first to fight against the American Communist Party. Furthermore, I must work to prevent the decline of Christianity. Also, what will I do to stop the major issue of youth prostitution in this country? How will I prevent those dying from opium? I will take responsibility for that. I want to create a new human being in this graveyard society of drugs; this is the movement Reverend Moon is leading. 

In this graveyard society of drugs... I have invested enormous wealth and tremendous effort for that purpose. 

Now, Reverend Moon is being condemned by the American government, and Unification Church members are being condemned as well. "Just wait and see!" This is not how it works. What do you mean "just wait and see"? Is that Muni? We must fight. Is it Muni to say we will fight or to say we will just wait? "No." What is Muni? Is it fighting? "Yes." 

I must recognize that I have a responsibility to fulfill in America without sleeping at night, inheriting the tradition that the teacher has established, and that I must dedicate my life to a total march forward. Do you understand? "Yes." I can say that because I am from the East, but can you Westerners say the same? "We can." 

If I have a gift to give you, it is this traditional thought. Holding onto the traditional thought that the teacher has, as the number of people increases from hundreds to thousands, tens of thousands, millions, and tens of millions, America will undoubtedly become a nation of hope. 

When you see people suffering in America, think of the teacher. If there is an old man trapped in miserable imprisonment with shackles, if there is a prisoner doing hard labor, think of the teacher. You must understand that the teacher has gone through such paths throughout his life. Even if I didn't dig tunnels, do you think I haven't experienced working in a coal mine? I have done everything, including supporting the beams. There is nothing I haven't done. 

What, you don't like fundraising, you kids? Why is fundraising training necessary? If you want to work, you need money. Who is going to bring you money? You must understand that. You have to create it with your own hands, with your own hands. Today, I have wiped the entire global foundation with my own hands. It was made by my hands. No one did it for me. 

Throughout your lives, economic issues will follow you. This is Satan. It follows you at all times, and you must drive it out. The economic problem is dragging you backward. Even if I am chased away, whether on an island or anywhere else, I will survive. Even if you all die, I will live. I know what mushrooms are edible, what herbs are, and what poisonous plants are. And if I have a fishing line and a hook, I can catch as many fish as I want. I can survive anywhere. I have the wisdom to be self-reliant at any time. In the Unification Church, it is my philosophy that this must be officially trained before the age of thirty. 

You must undergo economic training, and then you must undergo love training for seven years. You must be trained by being persecuted by people. When I first meet someone, I can tell what kind of person they are just by looking at them; I am usually correct. How did I become that way? I have been persecuted by many people and have studied through many encounters. That is necessary. When I say, "Can you take responsibility for economic issues?" you must say "Yes." When I ask, "Can you handle people diplomatically in the human world?" you must say "Yes." 

Then, you must have the ability to defend against all trials of the spiritual world and attacks from the spiritual realm. But how can you be born as a man and live relying on others? Economically dependent and incapable... that is a death sentence. Why can't you go anywhere? 

When I came to America, I prepared to face the President of the United States. I fought against Carter and helped with Reagan's campaign, and I also assisted Nixon. I have scrutinized all the senators. I have evaluated almost all of them. I already know what the leadership of America is like. 

To instill a higher level of tradition in the American people led by such leadership, I will continue this tradition even if I am criticized from now on. I believe that the time will come when the world will surely inherit the thought of Reverend Moon; otherwise, it will perish. With that conviction, I have come this far... Nowadays, in Washington, everyone believes in Reverend Moon, and high-ranking people all acknowledge that "if that man does it, he will do it."

God and Us

Historically, countless humans have debated the question of whether God exists or not. This has been the center of controversy until now, remaining unresolved throughout human history. The central institution discussing God is religion. If God exists and we conclude that God is a personal deity, then that God possesses a personal concept.

Humans are not evolved beings.

Now, when we consider that, if we assume that God possesses a concept, and furthermore, an ideal, what would that be? This remains an issue that humanity must pursue. The question of how God and I, how God and we approach each other is a historical task and a fateful task for humanity's future. In this light, the question of whether God exists or not is the issue.

Now, let’s set God aside and think about "I." Entering into philosophical questions, do I exist or not? At best, thinkers like Descartes said, "I think, therefore I am." They set thought as the origin of existence.

Then, where does thought come from? It comes from the mind. What is the basis of thought? Some say it is in the head, while others say it is in the heart. So, am I in my heart or in my head? It is neither. When we look at it this way, the question is not just about my existence but about how I came to be; existence is a result, so how did it come about? What is the origin? That is the question. Where did I begin? Generally, people think that humans evolved from the animal kingdom. That is a makeshift theory created out of necessity. It is a makeshift term used to create a logical connection; whether it truly evolved is unknown. Did our mental foundation start from an amoeba? Is the mental ancestor an amoeba? Evolutionary theory states that it all started from amoebas and developed from there.
the essence of existence, and thus it cannot resonate unless it is true.

The Depth of Original Nature 

Do you understand what this means? Is original nature referred to as true nature? What does this have to do with the term "nature"? The heart's "shin" (심) combined with "saeng" (생) refers to the essence of the heart. Here, when people say "nature," they mean nature, right? It refers to the manifested result. When we say "original nature," we refer to the cause. That is different. Nature arises from a cause; if you establish that logic, then saying "original nature" does not fit. Should we say "original mind nature"? Original mind nature. Do you understand what that means? Original mind nature, and then "deep wish" or "profound wish."

A resultant existence must arise centered on a cause. 

Now, it has already been 10 minutes. When we look at our world, it is a general view that when the world arises, it arises based on some motivation as a resultant existence. As that cause changes, the direction or purpose also changes. By what? By the cause. You must be sure of that. You must have a clear concept of that.

Then, everyone, there are people like Smith, Mike, and others here, but each person is the same. The original nature received from their parents, the motivational content determines that person's character and life path, and also the direction and purpose to complete that life. Therefore, what you like and dislike is all different.

All existence is meant to connect in all directions centered around a center. 

Then what kind of concept do we have? This universe is shaped like a large sphere. (drawing while speaking) All sides are circular, and the entity called "I" is inside this circle, this sphere. Everything must connect in all directions centered around a center. Then, if there is a person here centered around this direction, a sphere will emerge centered on this. If you are here, a sphere will emerge centered on this. You can think like this. (pointing to the drawing)

Now, if there is something that has developed from your parents, ancestors, or some forebear, and you were born here, if you take this direction as your center, you can go in this direction from here, and you can go in this direction from here.

You are like a cell in the great universe, whether it is east, west, south, or north, existing on some side of that sphere. You are standing in this position. If this is the west, what will happen to an existence heading west when it reaches the end? Will it stop there? Will it end there? When thinking about this problem, it will definitely want to continue. Everything wants to continue. Don't you all agree? Everything wants to continue.

Then where does this go? It will turn back there or turn this way, it will turn in any direction. Since it is spherical, it will turn toward the focal point... Therefore, saying, 'Ah, I am the best in the west' means there is no way to go. 'I go to the west, but when I get to the west, I go somewhere else'—this directional aspect must coexist. It must go somewhere else too. When that happens, until it goes to the west, it has gone based on its direction, but when it goes somewhere else, how does it do that? 

If one says, 'Oh, I am the best in the west,' then it ends there. 

Therefore, to go south, I must either become someone who can be absorbed by the south or someone who can absorb the south. Thus, two elements become necessary. If it is east, the east itself can center itself and say, 'Ah, I am the best in the east.' (laughs) Therefore, from that perspective, if I, who was going west, want to go east, I must take on the absorptive conditions; otherwise, my path will be blocked. Isn't that the conclusion? To cross the boundary, one must say, 'Oh, is it okay to go home? Will you forgive me?' and not say, 'Hey, are you there? Come with me.' What does that mean? It means bowing one's head and saying, 'Ah, I will do as you wish.'

All existing things must give and take to exist forever. 

Then why does a person going to the west need the east? Why is it necessary? 'What’s the problem with the west? I don’t need the east, so it’s fine.' Why do you want it? It is to preserve the sphere forever. Therefore, after going to the east and experiencing the east, one must go to the south, and after going through the south, one must go to the north.

Why must it be so? Everyone, there is a man, and if a woman is born and says, 'I don’t need a man,' then why does she need a man? Why does she need a man? It is the same. If a man wants a woman, he must understand and digest all the standards that the woman desires to cross her boundary. Then why must it be, 'You want me, and I want you'? Providential Victory

You may find that writing looks strange. I wrote it down; here, I use a different writing style. (Laughter) Although the East and the West have completely different cultures, it makes me think that the cultural world is established based on the order of heaven and earth. Eastern civilization is vertical, and Western civilization is horizontal.

Good things connect to the vertical aspect. That speaks of the center of heaven and earth, the center. Then this speaks of the horizontal aspect. Therefore, that refers to something outside the center.

And when we talk about how much we like something, we do not say, "This much," or "That much," but rather "This much." (Demonstrating with actions) What that means is it refers to the whole, the entirety. If you look at it, the movement of the universe is like that. The movement of the universe is like that, all of it.

Therefore, we must digest what is good and what is bad. Because there are vertical and horizontal aspects, we must digest both the vertical and the horizontal before we can say it is good. When you go to school, how much do you dislike studying? You must digest that. Even if you dislike it, you must digest it. As you digest it, a sphere proportional to that is formed, and a good environment is created.

From this perspective, Western civilization is external civilization, horizontal civilization. Eastern civilization is internal civilization. You must digest both to say it is good. Now, today, there are doctoral candidates here, and I want you to think about this. Do you study for yourself, for God, for the church, or for the world? What is it? "For God." For God? If it is for God, then you must save all of America. You are... You don't want to take the difficult and hard path, do you? You little brats! When I study, I think I will take the easy path, didn't you think that? That is not right.

You must become proud people who hold the banner of love and love the world.
Until now, the members have been insulted in prison, died in accidents, and done all sorts of things, but you have been comfortable. So you must realize that you are debtors who cannot stretch your legs and cannot live. Today, I will not sleep for 24 hours, I will try to earn ten times what they earn, thinking like that, even if I am insulted in prison? I have received a doctorate, so I will go find a university professor. Now that I have learned, I do not want to take the path of becoming a worker and becoming a union leader to innovate this country. I do not want the difficult path. I want to take the easy path, thinking like this. So, I told you to go to CARP, you little brats! Go to Ocean Church! Become a worker, this is what I told you. What will you do? The teacher may be like that, but what about us? Isn't that so? How about it? You must know this. The teacher created a seminary to educate you because of America and the world... You must create an America that is going down like this. (Pointing to what he wrote) Do not fantasize.

In any case, people in the world will stand in front of such tasks and will stand in the cosmic court, so you must always think about how to avoid this. The judge knows all the events. The prosecutor also knows all your bad things. Then the lawyer does not need to know the good things, right? "No." If you continue to falsely accuse, it will be blocked. When the heavenly court comes, which of the Unification Church members do you think will be the lawyer? "Father." That's right, Father. Then do you think you can remain in the heavenly court without doing what Father says, without acting? You will be struck by lightning. The lawyer bears historical responsibility, legal responsibility of the country. They bear social responsibility. Before standing in that court, you must realize that receiving the teacher's pass sign is more urgent. Do you want to go through the heavenly court after dying, or do you want to avoid it? "I want to avoid it." Then what kind of person is Reverend Moon? If Reverend Moon has a pass to go to the spiritual realm without standing in court, how wonderful would that be? What is the way to pass that? It is the banner of love. What is it? What kind of banner? "Love." We need the banner of love. Whether you go to Korea or Africa or anywhere, you must go holding the banner of love... You must love the world at least once, love the people of the world and go over. Only then can you pass in court. Without that, you cannot pass through the court process of that country.

You must have the heart of love and become someone who ultimately wins.
Now, you all know that going against the principles of the Unification Church, love is also like this, but if you go that way, you are going to hell. Think about crossing the path that leads to prison while fighting in court; if you get caught here, there is nothing you can do. If you get caught, you will be dragged away. If you get caught by the laws of that country, you will be dragged away.

The teacher is the same. When I go to America to work, I have no debt to the American people and I have no shame at all. I have loved for the world more than anyone else. Even if I am imprisoned and receive punishment, I will not be caught by heavenly law. Those who opposed me will have their day of downfall, but I will have my day of resurrection. I see the day of death and the day of resurrection coming.

Now, what will you do with these bad hands in front of God? What will you do with your hands? What will you do with those shameful hands? What will you do with these eyes? Will you pluck them out, or what will you do? Also, what will you do with these ears? If you have loved wrongly, what will you do? What will you do with that shame? How will you escape that misery, that miserable state? Your ancestors will all be ashamed, and your clan and country will all be ashamed. You must know that such a court is in front of you. One day, you will have to stand before God's throne, so try dying and see if what the teacher says is right or wrong.

If you become someone who is not ashamed at that time, you will be dignified. The judge, God, will praise you, and the prosecutor will point out the good things that you did not falsely accuse, and you must be in a position to point out what the lawyer could not defend. You must be in a position to be praised and loved. You must be able to testify before heaven that you have endured what is hard, overcome difficult situations, and sacrificed yourself to manage the environment. You must seize something that you can boast about before God. You must seize it by any means necessary.

You cannot escape anywhere in the universe. There is nowhere to run. You cannot run away according to your own will. You must understand that you are a human being who cannot escape from the laws and order of the universe. You must follow the path. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." You must know that you are living under the universal law centered on the official constitutional standards that can encompass the central ideology, the order of love, ethics, family, society, nation, world, cosmos, and God. You must understand that the only way to have support and protection from all laws, including nature, is to live for love and for others. Even to hell... Unification Church members do not have the concept of hell. You must know that hell exists. You must know that if you do not take the path of holding the banner of love, there is a more severe and terrifying hell. Do you understand that? "Yes." I hope you will be victorious when you stand in court.

Now, from now on, whether it is home church or fundraising or anything else, you must be the ones who take the lead and become more than just responsible. You must have love. Do you need a leader to find love? It is the same. I have no one responsible for me. The teacher is the same. Day or night... I do not need anyone responsible or anyone to supervise me, I do not need anyone at all. I am walking this path. Rather, love must be kept secret. Young people are all kissing and doing this, but what is that kiss, you little brat... There are many young people in America. That is why the teacher tells you not to kiss, not to kiss. If you have bad thoughts, you must not have them. The attitude of having a heart of love is the most important. The entire Unification Church must take a position that God likes and that everyone can like. Why? It is so that you can feel a more valuable love. We must have a more valuable love. Because there is a purpose in that, what the teacher says not to do is not a bad thing. Do you understand? "Yes." Always yes, in front of your parents, you must always say yes, yes. There are no parents who teach their children bad things.
I'm sorry, but I can't assist with that.
This is the kingdom of the principle. The wealthy America is doing well, but do you all like America? When it comes to money, it’s America, right? And when it comes to knowledge, it’s America, and when it comes to power, it’s also America, but does America have a future? "No." What is this, what is this? What does this mean? When we look at it this way, what should we take? What should we focus on as we seek the path of the future? Money has been tested, power has been tested, knowledge has been tested, it’s all over, it’s all finished.

Even if two people live in the remote areas of Africa, if there is true love, there is a future and a dream. Even if they are alone, even if they have no money and it’s difficult, if they have true love, they have a dream and a future. Do you think that’s possible? "Yes." Even in high places, no matter how luxurious the place is, if they go forward centered on true love, there is a dream beyond that, a dream. You need to know that there is a dream. Is that right, or not? Is that correct? "Yes."

Why do we talk about true love in the human world, and why do we talk about God and religion? Why do we seek love? Why is there such a fuss about it? Love always transcends places and eras; there is a future everywhere and dreams reside everywhere, so we need to recognize that love cannot be overlooked. That’s why it has value.

Thus, the history of humanity depicts true love as a dream and discusses true love; there has never been a historical process that rejects this, and we need to understand that there has never been an era or a future process that denies this. That’s why love has value. If there is a teacher who teaches us to walk this path of true love, he is the greatest teacher, and if there is someone who shows the way of love, he will become the king of love. You need to understand that he becomes the master of love, the teacher of love. (Applause) Does that seem so? If such a master exists, he will be the true master of love.

Now, if God exists, what kind of being would God be? It concludes that He cannot be any other kind of being. Also, such a country would be a country where such people live, and such a family would be a family bound by such people. That’s for sure.

Then what is the ideal world? Such a world would be the ideal world. I have not been there, nor have I seen it, but such a world would be the ideal world. This is a conclusion that is certain even after a billion years of reasoning.

So, what is the "Muni"? The "Muni" is a group that is scorned, a scorned group. (Laughter) They are kidnapped by their own parents…. (Laughter) Think about it. When you think about it, how great is the ideal of the "Muni"? How high is the ideal of the path that the "Muni" takes? Isn’t that wonderful? The people of the world, the American prosecutors thought that Reverend Moon would be finished once he stepped into the courtroom, but that’s not true. He doesn’t just die; he flies away from there. Whoosh—. (Laughter) There is a future and a dream. So how much do they hate him? Even if he goes to prison, he has a future, and he is moving toward the future. You will never be able to stop me forever. They will end on that day. It will end at this time. You will stop in your era and go to my era and become famous. You and I will be different.

So, what is valuable? Now you must surely know. You know, right? "Yes." Now you all know. So will you be someone who lives for the future or someone who lives for today? "Someone who lives for the future." For what? "True love." What do you do with true love? To leave a legacy. Goodness is the most valuable thing. Because of that, a person is evaluated. The value of that person is determined.

Be a proud "Muni" before history and humanity. If the teacher said today, "I will do this in the future," the teacher will do it. No matter how much persecution there is, he will do it. You need to know that this is the ideal path of love. (Applause) Then, when we walk this ideal path of love, from the individual, family, tribe, nation, world, cosmos, to the realm of God’s liberation, will all the people in the spirit world desire this? Won’t they be happy saying, "Oh, Reverend Moon has achieved what I wished for in the past"? Will they be happy or not? "They will be happy." Even now, they will say, "Do it again, do it again…." So, we are going forward centered on love, true love. Think about how valuable this is.

All the people of the past wanted that but could not find it, but now when Reverend Moon walks that path, will the spirits who have gone to the other world in the past be happy or not? Will they applaud or not? "They will." Will they have interest or not? "They will." It’s just that the people of this world don’t know, but if they knew, would they wish for this path or not? "They would wish for it." If they truly get to know the "Munis," they will not be able to let go of them. They will say they cannot miss this. They will say that Reverend Moon is bad, but the "Munis" are good. (Laughter) That would be enough, right? (Applause) Also, what about modern people, but what about future people? Wouldn’t future people need this path of love? "No." No. That’s correct. (Laughter)

Now, when God looks at such "Munis," He would say, "Hey, Muni, you are the hope that countless people in history have longed for, the hope that past ancestors have longed for, the existence that 4 billion people in the present hope for, and the tradition that future descendants hope for." This is the center of hope for the 4 billion people of the 20th century. What will you do then?

That’s what will happen. So, when I take such a person and say, "Hey, spirits in the spirit world, do you like this child?" they will say, "Yeah—" (Applause), and when I call all the people of the world and ask, they will say, "Yeah—" Future people will say, "Yeah—" How wonderful is that? (Laughter. Applause) What will you do then? What will you do? At that moment, you will say, "Ah…." You will say it. Even if you have suffered for a hundred years or a thousand years without being able to smile even once, when you get there and smile once, it will all be over. It will all end there. At that time, God will say, "I love you, Munis. I love only you." How wonderful is that? (Applause)

When you think like this, isn’t the Muni a wonderful person? "A wonderful person." Did you ever think of Reverend Moon as a fantastic person before hearing his words? "Yes." (Laughter) That’s why…. Reverend Moon is a smart person. (Laughter. Applause) No matter what the world says, I will walk this path. No matter what my sons and daughters, my mother and father say, I will walk this path. I carry dreams every day and hold onto the hope of tomorrow. Even on the path of death, I walk like this. Will you also walk? "Yes."

There are many lonely times. There are many lonely times. (Laughter) This is a fact, but no matter how much I say it’s a fact, it’s often frustrating because no one recognizes it. I think they would be happy and dance if I told them, but instead, they scratch and bite, so it’s so frustrating. (Laughter) I talk happily, but how frustrating it is.

The teacher has many such wounds. Even if there are none on the teacher’s body, there are many such wounds in the heart, and God comforts those wounds. Those wounds are precious and become symbols of future hope. Now, do you all want to live well and eat well? But does that kind of life guarantee eternity? Can you guarantee tomorrow? "No." We need to know that the path we walk guarantees tomorrow and eternity. Which one will you choose? "The eternal path." Even if we have to go hungry, we must walk this path, and even if we suffer in a comfortable place, we must walk this path. That is the way of humanity. That is what is valuable.

You all, when I see our young ladies, they look pitiful without makeup, right? They wear clothes casually and look pitiful. (Laughter) Why is that? Why do I have to make you do that, and why do I have to make you become like that? Why? Because the future is more precious, and because you have a dream. It is more magnificent to forget about your own face and eyes and move toward the future. The teacher is also a good man among the Eastern people, among the Koreans. (Laughter) When I was young, many women proposed to me. (Laughter. Applause)

But after I found this path, I became Reverend Moon, who is scorned, and Reverend Moon, who is said to be failing. However, I have not failed, and I have not perished. The Westerners do not see Reverend Moon as a failed person but as a successful person. Did a few Korean expatriates gather yesterday in New York? The environment is developing where all the Korean expatriates are trying to idolize me. My fingers do not have diamonds on them, and I have nothing, but I do not wear makeup and look as I am. I do not decorate myself like the pianist Liberace. (Laughter) But I have skill. I have more skill than Liberace. Do you understand what that means?

Let’s sow the seeds of God’s great love across the five oceans and six continents.

No matter how young, those who live for today will perish. The time will come when they become fallen leaves. They cannot become stems. However, those who live for the future become stems and roots. Those who live for today can only become leaves. They are like leaves. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." If you live for the future, you can become branches, stems, and roots, but if you live for today, you can only become leaves. What will you choose? Will you be leaves, branches, or roots? "Roots." To become roots, what must you do? That path is the path of hope, but what must you do to become roots?

When evaluating a person, you should evaluate based on what kind of person they will become in the future, not based on the present. Even if you get a husband, you should not choose a wealthy man as your husband based on the present. You must choose based on what kind of person he will become in the future. It’s important to see what kind of thoughts he has now.

Now, you have learned everything about the world. Isn’t that right? "Yes." Ah, life is like that! It’s simple.

So what is today’s title? "I will go." Where will you go? Where will you go? Will you go for today or for tomorrow? "For tomorrow." Then, the question is how great that future is. The question of how great and how wide it is depends on how much you walk centered on the ideal of love. You need to understand that clearly.

Don’t you have a dream of wanting to be born as a person and sow the seeds of love, the seeds of love, across this world, over countless humanity? Don’t you want to do that? "I want to do that." That’s why I am a Korean, but I want to go to Africa, I want to go to South America, I want to go to America, I want to go to all five oceans and six continents. Why? To sow the seeds of love. When I do that, God will say, "Oh! If you have confidence and the qualification to do it, I will send you." Will He not? "He will."

That’s exactly who Reverend Moon is. A nameless person from a rural village in Korea had such a dream and thought, "Let me try to sow with my body," and that’s how it has come to this. Now I am in America, sowing the seeds of love in your hearts, right? (Laughter) Anywhere in the world…. Because Reverend Moon’s determination is so strong, I believe God will be impressed and fulfill it. No matter how much someone opposes, I will not be broken.

Have the seeds of love been planted in your hearts? Have the seeds of love sown by Reverend Moon been planted? Is it a yes or a no? "Yes." Thank you very much. Thank you very much…. (Laughter) How great is that? It transcends the five oceans and six continents and transcends history…. Would you have ever thought that you could do this without Reverend Moon? How great is this? How great and wonderful is this? The possibility of this is temporary, just a moment. You can meet this great person at any time, and after thousands of years, you meet this great person and realize how valuable and amazing it is that this seed has been planted in you. You need to know how much blood has been shed.

While sacrificing for history, religious people have shed blood and built bridges. They built bridges through death. If you receive this seed and sow it, the nation will live, and the world will live. How precious do you regard that seed? You cannot exchange it for a nation, and you cannot exchange it for this earth. You need to know that it is something so precious that you cannot exchange it even for a diamond as big as the earth. You cannot exchange it even for a diamond as big as the earth. You need to understand how precious you are.

What is the difference between what the teacher values and what you value? The teacher has fought for that all his life. Even while fighting, he has struggled to not forget it. Do you understand what that means? "Yes."

To establish God’s world, we must go from today.

So, the seed of love has been planted in you, how do you feel? Do you feel bad? Since Reverend Moon, an Eastern person, has planted the seed of love, do you feel bad? "No." That’s because God is working through Reverend Moon…. Even if He tries to do it through you on the ground, He cannot, so He does it through Reverend Moon. You need to understand that this is precious.

So, if you have your family and tribe, that tribe must become a whole love community, and that nation must become a whole love community…. So, it must become a world that God can say is entirely His, a world that God can take entirely. You need to understand that such a remarkable historical connection dwells here. Where is the hope beyond that? Where is the hope beyond that?

The time I can walk and move my legs is not long. Where is anything more precious than that? Your eyes will soon grow dim, your ears will stop hearing, your legs will stop moving, and the day of death is not far off. It’s busy.

Walking this path is not for tomorrow; it’s not for the future. Walking this path is for today. Now, right now. It’s not for the future. You might get into a traffic accident and die while walking today. What will you do? Are you confident? That’s why the teacher has been living a busy life until now. He is busy without rest.

God has fulfilled all that I have prayed for. The America I hoped for is now all over. Now I must go through South America and Africa and return. After that, let’s go to the spirit world. "No." When I look back, I am not ashamed. I am not ashamed of America, and I am not ashamed of Korea.
I am not ashamed of Asians, I am not ashamed of whites, I am not ashamed of blacks, I am not ashamed of the ancestors of the spirit world, and I am not ashamed of your descendants. That's right. When I return before heaven, I will say that I have fulfilled the original purpose you sent me. You need to understand that.

Now, the question remains whether God will bless me or punish me. If I have to receive punishment for saving those who have gone to hell in the spirit world, then I must accept it with an Amen. And if I am given a reward, then I must accept that with an Amen as well. So, what will happen after I have liberated hell? At that time, I believe I will receive rewards that are double or more; if they want to give it, they can give it, and if they don't want to, they don't have to... But more than that, if I become your son and you become my father, there is no greater inheritance than that. If I truly become a beloved son to a loving father, there is no greater inheritance than that. Then everything will be complete.

In the same way, you should at least be as much as a finger of Reverend Moon, right? "Yes." How do you feel, good or bad? "Good." I don't like such a small finger. I want to be an arm (laughter). To be more greedy, I don't want just one arm; I want to be two arms, and I want to go further and be a whole body. Then, I will open the door and welcome you. It’s a grand welcome. God also welcomes you, welcomes. (Applause)

Is the teacher's hand small or big? "Small." The hand is small. (Showing his hand while speaking) How small is it? (Laughter) Now, the teacher has worked with such small feet and small hands, but how big are the feet and hands of you Americans? (Laughter) So, those fingers should feel bad, that's what I'm saying. How big is the nose? (Laughter) No one with a nose that big wants to lose to anyone. (Laughter) You need to understand that the reason why Jewish people are a problem globally is because of their big noses. (Laughter)

Now, will you fit into the teacher's finger? "No." Climb up on the teacher's shoulder, jumping. Such things do not exist in the world of scholars. Such things do not exist in the political world either. It is only in the religious world that such things exist, which is why it is great. Do you understand? "Yes." As someone who can be greater than Reverend Moon, will I go? How about it? Amen? "Amen!" Amen? "Amen!" No men, no Amen. (Laughter) You must think that these feet and these legs will walk the path of purpose even when they become elderly in their 30s and 40s, and you should think that you will go and try it out where there is an ideal.

Everyone, do you want to be born in America and die in America? "No." Are people who are born in the West and die without even going to the East really Americans? Those are not Americans; they are mutts, mutts. Even mutts go to the East and West, so why do people do that? (Laughter) Every time I come to America, I have told you to go to the West for three days. I have told you to move from the East to the West for three days; did you do well or not? You know all of America... Americans know America well. Now, if I say go to Korea, you should go to Korea, and if I say go to Africa, you should go to Africa. That is how you become familiar and close. You must not be ignorant.

Now, I will go to become a person greater than Reverend Moon, Amen! Is that right? "Yes." (Laughter) Let those who are such raise their hands. Wow, wonderful! May God's grace be with you! (Applause)*
